						<h2 class="h2">Cocktail hours</h2><div class="wysiwyg"><p><span class="size-h4">Cocktail hours is our way of celebrating the end of the hard day. With a selection of signature cocktails and a menu full of nibbles, fall into our lounges and let the day drift away.</span></p>

</section><section id="a-heritage-as-rich-as-our-flavours" class="content-area-x2 background-primary" data-row-type="content_row_no_image" data-row-index="row-5">
		<div class="grid-container position_relative">
		<div class="grid-x align-center">
			<div class="cell">
				<div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-padding-y  align-center  text-center">
					<div class="cell  large-10 xlarge-8">
											
						<h2 class="h2">a heritage as rich as our flavours</h2><div class="wysiwyg"><p><span class="size-h4">Parlour is based in the historic former Hotel Acton, which was designed by Commonwealth Architect John Smith Murdoch as a replica of the Hotel Kurrajong in Barton. The Hotel Acton’s first guests arrived to celebrate the opening of Parliament House on 9 May 1927. Since then, the building was home to everything from the Patent Office and the Institute of Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander Affairs to the AFP. In fact, part of the Mabo legislation was drafted between these four walls. So, when you walk through our doors, you’re stepping into an integral part of Australian history.</span></p>
<p><span class="size-h4">Today, we’re proud to add to the building’s wealth of stories and occasions. Come taste forward-thinking food flavoured by hints of an eclectic and wonderful past.</span></p>
</div>							
												
											</div>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>

		<script>		
		//event listener: DOM ready
		function addLoadEvent(func) {
			var oldonload = window.onload;
			if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
				window.onload = func;
			} else {
				window.onload = function() {
					if (oldonload) {
						oldonload();
					}
					func();
				}
			}
		}
		//call plugin function after DOM ready
		addLoadEvent(function(){
			outdatedBrowser({
				bgColor: '#f25648',
				color: '#ffffff',
				lowerThan: 'borderImage',
				languagePath: 'https://parlourdining.com.au/wp-content/themes/parlour/assets/js/lang/en.html'
			})
		});
		</script>
